24/05/23, 12:50â€¯pm - +91 90150 92143: Dear All,

Greetings of the day!!
The Department of CSE-DS & Department of CSE-AIML in association with Institution's Innovation Council - ABESEC are organizing "The Shark Pitch'23" on 29th May 2023.  


Details of Event are as follows:
Title: The Shark Pitch'23

Objective: The primary objective of this competition is to encourage and recognize innovative solutions that contribute to the development of a sustainable future. Participants will have the opportunity to present their business ideas or technological innovations, focusing on addressing environmental, social, or economic challenges within industries such as energy, transportation, agriculture, waste management, water conservation, and beyond.

Competition category: 

Category A: App/Website + Business Model Canvas*

Category B: Project/Product + Business Model Canvas*

Competition Structure: 

Registration and Initial Idea Submission: Interested individuals or teams will register for the competition, outlining their business idea or innovation in a concise manner. This will include a summary of the problem being addressed, the proposed solution, and its potential impact. 
Selection and Mentoring: A panel of experts and industry professionals will evaluate the submissions and select the most promising ideas. These selected participants will receive mentorship from experienced professionals who will guide them in refining their ideas, developing business models, and crafting compelling pitches. 
Pitching and Finalist Selection: Participants will present their ideas in front of a distinguished panel of judges, potential investors, and industry leaders. The presentations will be followed by a Q&A session, where participants will have the opportunity to defend and elaborate on their ideas. The judges will evaluate the presentations based on criteria such as innovation, feasibility, potential impact, and scalability, among others. 
Funding and Support: The winners of the competition will receive various forms of support, including financial assistance, access to a network of investors, business development resources, and ongoing mentorship. This support will enable them to turn their ideas into tangible products or services and launch their ventures successfully. 

Competition Benefits: 
Recognition and Exposure: Participants will gain visibility among industry leaders, potential investors, and the broader public, enhancing their professional profiles and fostering future collaborations. 
Mentorship and Guidance: Competitors will have the opportunity to work closely with experienced mentors who will provide valuable insights, guidance, and industry connections to help refine their ideas and business strategies. 
Funding Opportunities: Winners will secure financial support to bring their ideas to fruition, helping them overcome initial funding challenges and accelerate the growth of their ventures. 
Networking and Partnerships: Participants will have access to a network of like-minded individuals, investors, and industry experts, fostering potential collaborations and partnerships that can fuel their ventures' success. 

Competitions outcomes: 

Participating in a business idea competition can enhance critical thinking skills, leadership abilities, poise, and professionalism, which are highly valuable qualities in the job market. 
Competing in a business idea competition can have a significant impact on boosting confidence and overcoming fears associated with presenting ideas and pitching to a panel of judges or potential investors. 
By participating in a business idea competition, individuals not only have the opportunity to learn about successful entrepreneurs and their business strategies, planned execution, and valuation methods, but also gain exposure to business jargon and terminology commonly used in the entrepreneurial ecosystem. 

Registration details:  

Team Size: Individual or in a team of 5 students (maximum) 

Online registration link: https://forms.office.com/r/yB9CMLCQ1w

Last date: 25th May 2023 

Award & Recognition for winners: Top three participants will get the Certificate and trophies.

*Business Model Canvas: The Business Model Canvas is a strategic management template used for developing new business models and documenting existing ones. 

Date and Time: 29th May, 2023 || 09:00 AM - 05:00 PM

Audience: Interested students

Venue: Seminar Hall-1, Raman Block, ABESEC

Greetings of the day!

We are delighted to inform you that the departments of CSE-AIML and CSE-DS, in collaboration, are organizing a project day named "Nirmaan: Ignite, Innovate and Inspire!" on June 5, 2023. Nirmaan aims to provide a platform to showcase your innovative projects, receive mentorship for project completion, and participate in a stimulating problem-solving competition.

Objectives of the event:
1. Encourage students to complete and present their ongoing projects.
2. Provide mentorship and guidance to those who require assistance in completing their projects.
3. Promote interdisciplinary collaboration and knowledge exchange.
4. Foster problem-solving skills and critical thinking in a competitive environment.

Expected Outcomes:
1. Receive valuable feedback and suggestions for improving your projects.
2. Expand your professional network by connecting with like-minded individuals.
3. Gain recognition for your innovative ideas and contributions.

Benefits:
1. Get personalized guidance and support from experienced mentors to overcome project challenges and ensure successful completion.
2. Showcase your work to a diverse audience, including faculty members, industry experts, and peers.
3. Hone your presentation and communication skills by explaining your projects and solutions concisely and effectively.
4. Stand a chance to win exciting prizes and gain recognition for your achievements.

Roadmap:
1. Submission of Project & Problem Statements: All the participants need to submit precise problem statements of their respective projects.
Date:30/05/2023

2. Delegation of essentials: Participants need to submit a video and flex presenting the gist of the problem statement.
Date:01/06/2023

3. Offline Mentorship & Problem Statements release for Solution Sprint : Guidance will be provided for project completion and feature addition. Problem Statements for Solution Sprint will be revealed.
Date : 03/06/2023

4. Final Exhibition:
I. Project Presentation : Presentation of project in accordance to problem statement submitted
Timing - 9 AM - 1 PM
ii. Solution Sprint: Demonstration of idea formulated for Mini Hackathon problem statements
Timing - 2 PM - 5 PM
Date: 05/06/2023

Recognition and Awards:
Top 5 teams from 3rd year and top 8 teams from 2nd year will get exciting prizes.

Dear students,

Greetings of the Day!!

In response to the positive feedback received from the students in Phase 1 (Simplifi Lab) , we will be proceeding towards Phase 2.

The Phase-2 program is a piad program and only for interested students with a nominal fee of Rs. 1000. It will have 8 to 10 classes. These classes will be conducted in blended mode (online and offline) and will be taken by company officials with hands-on in college premises.

A glimpse of Phase 2 (a comprehensive course on React.js and Angular):

            Specially designed 08 modules, spread over nearly 12 classes only.
            Training by industry professionals.
            Hands-on in the college.
            Project based learning.

I _____________,Student of B.Techâ€¦â€¦â€¦â€¦/MCA/M.Techâ€¦â€¦â€¦â€¦..(Sem/Branch) solemnly pledge to uphold the dignity, safety, and well-being of every member of this institugtion. I recognize the harmful consequences of ragging, and I am committed to creating a campus environment that is free from any form of harassment, intimidation, or bullying.

I pledge to:

1. Treat my fellow students, juniors, and seniors with respect and dignity, irrespective of their background, beliefs, or appearances.

2. Foster an atmosphere of inclusivity and understanding, where every individual can freely express themselves without fear of ragging or discrimination.

3. Refrain from participating in, promoting, or supporting any activity that can be construed as ragging. I will actively prevent and discourage any instances of ragging.

4. Extend my support and assistance to any student who may be subjected to ragging, ensuring they feel safe to report incidents without hesitation.

5. Immediately report of  any ragging incidents or suspicious activities to the appropriate authorities, ensuring the prompt action necessary to prevent further harm.

6. Empower myself and my fellow students to stand up against ragging, fostering a culture where no one feels powerless or isolated.

7. Engage in positive interactions and constructive conversations that contribute to a harmonious and nurturing educational environment.

8. I Understand that ragging is a punishable offense under the law and within the institution's rules and regulations. I acknowledge that my actions have consequences.

By taking this pledge, I commit to being a responsible and empathetic member of this college community. I stand united with my fellow students, faculty, and staff to ensure a campus that promotes growth, learning, and friendship while condemning all forms of ragging.

I hereby solemnly affirm my dedication to the principles of this pledge.

23/11/23, 1:38â€¯pm - +91 90150 92143: Student 2 -Wheeler Parking Policy

Eligibility:

a. This policy is applicable to all enrolled students who commute to campus on two-wheelers.

b. Students must meet the following requirements:

i) Possess a valid driver's license, ii) Have a proper helmet, iii) Be at least 18 years old.

Parking Guidelines:

1. Students must park their motorcycles exclusively in designated motorcycle parking areas designated by the campus administration, including:

i) Area A: Motorcycle Parking Zone adjacent to Vishwakarma Block.

ii) Area B: Parking Zone adjacent to the aforementioned marked area.

2. Ensure that motorcycles are parked in an organized manner to allow easy access and movement for other motorcycles and pedestrians.

3. Students are responsible for securely locking and safeguarding their motorcycles against theft. The College Authorities are not liable for any loss of belongings left in the parking area or on the vehicle.

Compliance and Enforcement:

1. Non-compliance with the motorcycle parking guidelines may lead to penalties, such as warnings, fines, or the revocation of the parking sticker.

2. Campus security personnel and designated authorities will monitor motorcycle-parking areas and enforce policy compliance.

Application Process:

1. To obtain a motorcycle-parking sticker, students must complete the Google Form provided by the Admin Office, which will be sent on their email address.

2. The application form will necessitate the following details:

a) Full name.

b) Student Admission Number.

c) Contact information (phone number, email address).

d) Upload the bike's Registration Certificate.

If the student is using a motorcycle owned by a relative or another individual, a separate

Certificate be attached, providing full details of the student and clearly stating that

the student will use the vehicle.

e) Upload a valid driver's license.

3. After submission of the Google form, the Admin Office will review the application and

verify the provided information.

4.Once the application is verified, the Admin Office will notify the student via email regarding

the availability of the approved parking sticker.

5.Students should collect the parking sticker from the Admin Office and prominently display it on their vehicle in a visible location, preferably on the front mudguard.

6. The sticker is non-transferable and be used only on the registered student's motorcycle.

7. In case of loss of sticker Rs.50/- will be charged for issue of duplicate parking sticker.

By adhering to this revised application process, students can efficiently obtain their parking stickers and ensure compliance with the campus motorcycle parking regulations.

Chief Administrative Office

BNY Mellon Code Divas Diversity Challenge
BNY Mellon invites you to participate in the transformative challenge - Code Divas. Our commitment to Diversity, Equity and Inclusion is at forefront, fostering an inclusive environment where collaboration thrives. Together, we aim to break barriers and enhance transparency in the investment lifecycle, shaping a future that embraces innovation and diversity.

Embrace the opportunity to be part of Code Divas, now in its fourth edition with a renewed commitment to empowering women in technology. If you're a passionate and talented woman engineer aspiring to leave your mark in the financial industry, BNY Mellon Technology, India is the place for you. Join an incredible team dedicated to shaping the future of finance and don't miss this chance to showcase your skills and make a meaningful impact.

What is your benefit?
Code Divas offers you more than just a challenge; it opens doors to exciting possibilities. By participating, you stand a chance to secure a spot in our interview process for tech internships and full-time positions. Elevate your career journey with a valuable advantage and take the first step towards your dream career with BNY Mellon. Apply now and be part of a program that not only values your skills but celebrates the diversity you bring to the table. Join us in this Journey of innovation, collaboration, and empowerment.

Eligibility criteria & conditions of participation
1.	Female candidates & those who identify as female only are eligible to participate.
2.	BE/B. Tech. (full-time programs only).
a.	2024 graduates, if selected through interview process will be considered for a full time role.
b.	2025 graduates, if selected through interview process will be considered for summer internship role (May 2024 to July 2024).
c.	2026 graduates, if selected through the challenge and scored above cut off will be considered for an interviewing opportunity for internship role (May 2025 to July 2025).
3.	Students with CGPA above 7.5 only can apply. Participants are requested to convert your university percentage accordingly.
4.	The competition is open to students of private and government universities in India.
5.	Participating students should not have any current/active backlogs in any subject at the time of participation.
6.	Each round qualifies you to the next round of the process.
7.	The organizer reserves the right to amend or change the rules of participation or to cancel the competition without giving any reason or prior notice.
8.	All costs related to the preparation (if any) shall be borne by the applicable participant.
9.	Participants, by agreeing to these conditions of participation, consent to the publication of their names in connection with the announcement of the winner of the competition.
10.	Participants retain all intellectual property rights in and to their submissions. By agreeing to these conditions of participation, the participants confirm that they have all necessary rights and authority to agree to these conditions.
11.	Students acknowledge and agree that any flagged/suspected with plagiarism in the submissions made will lead to disqualification from the competition.
12.	Please reach out to support@hackerearth.com for all inquiries concerning the competition.
13.	Winners of the competition will be announced by BNY Mellon campus team

Challenge Format
Round 1: The Passionate Programmer: Your opportunity to show us your true passion & agility for technology & programming. This round will comprise of 3 Programming Questions to be solved within two-and-a-half hours using a programming language of your choice.

Tech-It-Out with BNY Mellon Employees & Leaders: Check the announcements section on this page for more details after Round 1 

Round 2: The 10X Engineer: Congratulations on demonstrating your zeal for programming in Round 1. This round 2, is intended to push you further testing your core software engineering skills &, fundamentals. Are you up for a more exciting challenge? 
â€¢	1 Programming Question in specific language- Java 8 (and above) OR Python
â€¢	1 SQL Question.

Note:
â€¢	Participation for Round 2 is by invitation only.
â€¢	You will require a webcam to be able to take this test (for both rounds). Please have a functional webcam-enabled and grant access to the pop-up on the browser.

07/02/24, 1:43â€¯pm - +91 84477 68492: Dear All
kindly refer following messsge regarding  proposals submission for funding under UBA SEGs 
 
Greetings from Unnat Bharat Abhiyan, A flagship Program of MoE (GoI), Nationally Coordinated by IIT Delhi.

We would like to inform you that we have opened the Subjet Expert Group (SEG) portal for the second round of proposals submission for funding under UBA SEGs from 26th January to 9th February 2024.

Please note that currently the portal is open for submission of proposals by participating institutes under 5 SEGs who have completed the process of evaluation in the first round and the details are given below:

1. Capacity Building, Strategy for Convergence and Implementation of Various Govt. Schemes - Dr. R. Ramesh, NIRD&PR Hyderabad

2. â Ethos in Technical Institutions - Prof. Anand B. Rao, IIT Bombay

3. Rural Energy Systems - Prof. P.M.V. Subbarao, IIT Delhi

4. Sanitation & Solid Waste Management- Prof. Indumathi Nambi, IIT Madras

5. Sustainable Agriculture System - Dr. R.N. Padaria, IARI New Delhi

PIs can access the Unnat Bharat Abhiyan website using the following direct login link: https://unnatbharatabhiyan.gov.in/pi/login then can navigate to the "Apply for SEG Proposal" tab located on the left side of their dashboard/screen and can select the SEG of their interest to submit the proposal under 2 categories; namely Technology Development and Technology Customization.

Technology Development: This category involves the submission of proposals where the technological interventions are already developed in the lab and they are now ready to disseminate in the field/ rural areas. The technological interventions should be the solution to the problem identified in the initial baseline survey in that particular area and the fund cap under this category is â‚¹1,00,000. PIs should ensure that the solutions submitted by them are fully sustainable, innovative, implementable and scalable, also, PIs should ensure the sustainability of the project after the completion of the project. There is no scope for mere lab projects or proto-types and all solutions and should have been tested at the field level and it should be demand driven.
Technology Customization: This category involves the technological interventions which are already available in the market but require some alterations/modifications to benefit the rural population according to their geographical locations. The proposal should specify a time target for specific outputs. The fund cap for this category is â‚¹50,000 and PIs should ensure the sustainability of the project after the completion of the project.  
Note: Long-term research projects/fellowships of any kind, cost on Ph.D. programs, setting up laboratories/centres, exhibitions and similar events, workshops and capital/construction are not available through the Unnat Bharat Abhiyan program, as the mandate of UBA SEG is to provide the financial support for technical interventions in the fields ( In UBA connected village) not for R&D.
 

With Regards,
Unnat Bharat Abhiyan Office, NCI - IIT Delhi
A Flagship Program of the Ministry of Education, GoI

For More Details,
Pl. contact, 
Dr. Rohit Rastogi (8076772048), Faculty-CSE & 
Nodal Officer, UBA-Wing of ABESEC
A Block-First Floor

Department of Computer Science of Engineering â€“ AIML is organizing a guest lecture on â€œNovelty and Intellectual Property (IP) Generation Opportunities in the Age of AI & MLâ€ on 29th June, 2024 from 10:30 AM to 11:30 AM for all faculty members &  students of Computer Science of Engineering â€“ AIML.    
 
Brief  about the Session: 
 
The rapid advancements in Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Machine Learning (ML) are transforming various industries, creating unprecedented opportunities for innovation and the generation of intellectual property (IP). This lecture will explore the avenues for novelty and IP generation in the context of AI and ML, identifying key areas where these technologies are driving transformative changes. It probes into the types of IP that can be generated, the challenges in protecting AI and ML innovations, and the strategies for maximizing IP value. Furthermore, the lecture will discuss the role of interdisciplinary collaboration and policy frameworks in fostering a robust IP ecosystem for AI and ML advancements in academia.

Eligibility & Team Rules:
â€¢	This competition is open to students pursuing B.Tech/B.E./M.Tech/M.S or related Engineering Programs across ALL Engineering Colleges in India (Batch 2025,2026, 2027 & 2028)
â€¢	Students must register in teams of 1 to 3 members
â€¢	Cross-Specialization teams are eligible

â€¢	The participating students can be from any specialization
â€¢	One person cannot be a member of more than one team
â€¢	Any deviation from the above will result in immediate disqualification of the entire team
Stages:
The Software Development Track will have 3 elimination levels to test your technical, analytical, and ideation skills before the National Finale where the Finalists will get to present their solutions to the Panel of Domain Experts at Flipkart.
Level 1 - E-Commerce & Tech Quiz:
â€¢	All registered teams will have to take an online quiz
â€¢	It is mandatory for all team members to attempt the quiz round
â€¢	A team will be scored based on the average marks of the team members attempting the quiz round
â€¢	All teams will be taking this quiz simultaneously during the quiz window
â€¢	Every participant will be ranked on Accuracy + Speed (Time Taken) + Start Time i.e., if two teams have the same score, then the team that started and finished earlier will be ranked higher
â€¢	Participating teams will move on to the next level based on their performance in this assessment
â€¢	It will be based on E-Commerce Trivia (Reference: https://stories.flipkart.com) and Tech (Technology Awareness + Techstack & Computer Science Fundamentals)
Level 2 - Submission Round:
â€¢	Shortlisted teams from Level 1 will have to participate in Level 2
â€¢	Teams will have to submit solutions for their preferred problem statement
â€¢	You'll be able to make submissions until the deadline for this level anytime during the challenge window
â€¢	The candidates can compress their videos here
â€¢	The expectation at this level will be to submit the functional proof of concept along with the demo video and code submission
â€¢	Participating teams in this level will move on to the next level based on their performance
Level 3 - The National Finale: In the final level of the GRiD, finalists will be invited to showcase their solutions to the panel of domain experts at Flipkart.
What's at stake? - Rewards and Prizes:
Attractive prizes to be won along with the opportunity to be a part of the hiring process for Tech Internships & Full-Time Roles (Internship Stipend: INR 1,00,000 per month; SDE-1 Role Compensation: INR 32 LPA)
â€¢	Winners get EGVs worth INR 1,00,000*
â€¢	First Runners-Up Get EGVs worth INR 75,000*

â€¢	Level 1 qualifying teams
â€¢	Finalists

â€¢	Top teams who qualify for level 2 will get a chance to be a part of the hiring process for Internship and full-time tech roles at Flipkart
â€¢	Teams who reach the finale get a PPI for a software tech role (Internship/full-time)

11/09/24, 12:54â€¯pm - +91 90150 92143: Dear Students,   
  
Greetings of the day!!!   
  
We are in planning to organize the Smart India Hackathon-2024 (Internal) soon in the campus. The primary objective of this hackathon is to select final 30 Teams (25 Final + 5 Reserve) including Software and Hardware edition. The 25 winning teams will be official entry from ABESEC in the main SIH 2024 (National Level). Also to identify potential solutions that have capability to be converted as a startup through the Incubation support.

Early steps required before register for the internal hackathon:
1) Select the right problem statement (Visit https://sih.gov.in/sih2024PS).
2) Team formation (6 members including minimum 1 girl candidate, higher the girls increase your chance of selection with good technical and communication skills).
3) Innovation solution development against the problem 

Background: 
Smart India Hackathon (SIH) is a premier nationwide initiative designed to engage students in solving some of the most pressing challenges faced in everyday life. Launched to foster a culture of innovation and practical problem-solving, SIH provides a dynamic platform for students to develop and showcase their creative solutions to real-world problems. By encouraging participants to think critically and innovatively, the hackathon aims to bridge the gap between academic knowledge and practical application. Visit https://www.sih.gov.in/ for more details. 
 
Three Steps for Idea Submission:   
1) Register online at https://forms.office.com/r/B0CGFxTyp8 till 11th September 2023, 9pm.        
2) Participate in Internal Hackathon to be held in college.   
3) Submit your details on SIH official portal through SPOC-ABESEC, if you are among top 25 winners <This message was edited>

04/10/24, 4:04â€¯pm - +91 87076 60239: Dear students, 

*It is once again reminded you all that kindly follow the discipline rules of the college*. 

 *It is mandatory to wear identity card*

*From monday onwards no student will be allowed in the class or lab without id card*

1. String of College Identify Card is available in the accounts section with a payment of Rs. 30/-.

2. The plastic holder of College Identity Card is available in the accounts section with a payment of Rs.20/-.

*Process for getting duplicate College Identify Card*

1. Students who have lost their College Identify Card are to apply for a duplicate Identity Card in an application form available in the college stationery outlet.
2. Students are to lodge an online FIR about the loss of their Identify Card.
3. Then the student has to deposit Rs.200/- in the accounts section and along with the application form, the student has to attach the fee receipt, a copy of online FIR and a passport size photograph in the office of the Registrar. 
4. The office of the Registrar would immediately issue a temporary Identity Card and within ten working days, a permanent Identify Card would be issued by the office of the Registrar. 

If any student having any type of issue or facing any problem, he/she can come to my cabin. 

Attend all the classes in proper uniform and I'D card.
Class timing is 8:50 AM, so be on time and after 8:50 you will not be allowed in the class/lab.
 
Regards
AIML Proctor
